<div disp-attr='NSJ' style="position: relative;" class="g_comp">


<script type="text/javascript">
/**
* 관련검색어 pc용 스크립트
* 바로가기 니즈 키워드 (기준 CTR 50% 이상) 인 경우 관련검색어 노출을 확대해서(3줄 펼치기 형태) 관련검색어 클릭을 높인다 - 2013.11.5 로직 삭제
*/
(function (jq) {
C.netizenColl = C.netizenColl || {};
C.netizenColl = {
applyTopBottom: function (position) {
var NetizenToggle = function (type) {
this.type = (type) ? type : "";
this.btnEl = jq("#netizen_more_btn_" + type);
this.btnTextEl = jq("#netizen_more_btn_" + type + " span.ico_rwd");
this.listsWrapper = jq("#netizen_lists_" + this.type);
this.lists = jq("#netizenColl_" + this.type + " .list_keyword span.wsn");
this.listKeywords = jq("#netizenColl_" + this.type + " .list_keyword span.wsn a.keyword");
this.tab = this.listsWrapper.data("w");
this.listFoldClass = (this.tab == "img") ? "type1" : "type2";   /* 이미지는 기본 1줄, 나머지는 기본 2줄 노출 */
this.listOpenClass = "type3";   /* 쵀대 4줄 노출 */
};
NetizenToggle.prototype = {
init: function () {
if (this.btnEl.length > 0) {
this.setListType();
this.btnEl.unbind("click").bind("click", jq.proxy(this.toggle, this));
this.listKeywords.unbind("click").bind("click", jq.proxy(this.sendLog, this));
jq(window).resize(jq.proxy(this.setListType, this));
}
},
setListType: function () {
var lineCount = this.getLineCount();
switch (lineCount) {
case 1:
this.setBtnStatus("more", "hide");
this.listsWrapper[0].className = "list_keyword";
break;
case 2:
if (this.tab == "img") {
if (this.listsWrapper.hasClass("type3")) {
this.setBtnStatus("fold", "show");
this.listsWrapper[0].className = "list_keyword " + this.listOpenClass;
} else {
this.setBtnStatus("more", "show");
this.listsWrapper[0].className = "list_keyword " + this.listFoldClass;
}
} else {
this.setBtnStatus("more", "hide");
this.listsWrapper[0].className = "list_keyword";
}
break;
case 3:
case 4:
if (this.tab == "img") {
if (this.listsWrapper.hasClass("type1") || this.listsWrapper.hasClass("type2")) {
this.setBtnStatus("more", "show");
this.listsWrapper[0].className = "list_keyword " + this.listFoldClass;
} else {
this.listsWrapper[0].className = "list_keyword " + this.listOpenClass;
}
} else {
this.setBtnStatus("more", "show");
this.listsWrapper[0].className = "list_keyword " + this.listFoldClass;
}
break;
}
},
setBtnStatus: function (opt1, opt2) {
if (opt1 == "more") {
this.btnEl.removeClass("fold");
this.btnTextEl.text('더보기');
} else if (opt1 == "fold") {
this.btnEl.addClass("fold");
this.btnTextEl.text('접기');
}
if (typeof(opt2) != "undefined") {
if (opt2 == "hide") {
jq(this.btnEl).addClass("hide");
} else if (opt2 == "show") {
jq(this.btnEl).removeClass("hide");
}
}
},
toggle: function (e) {
var lineCount = this.getLineCount();
var logData = this.btnEl.data("log");
if (lineCount > 1) {
if (this.btnEl.length > 0) {
if (this.btnEl.hasClass("fold")) {
this.setBtnStatus("more");
this.listsWrapper[0].className = "list_keyword " + this.listFoldClass;
smartLog(this.btnEl, logData + "&e=2", e);
} else {
this.setBtnStatus("fold");
this.listsWrapper[0].className = "list_keyword " + this.listOpenClass;
smartLog(this.btnEl, logData + "&e=1", e);
}
}
}
},
getLineCount: function () {
var list = this.lists[this.lists.length - 1];
var top = jq(list).position().top;
var lineHeight = 25;
var margin = 5;
/* 한 줄이 25 */
if (top >= lineHeight * 3 && top >= lineHeight * 3 - margin) {  /* 70~75 */
return 4;
} else if (top >= lineHeight * 2 && top >= lineHeight * 2 - margin) { /* 45~50 */
return 3;
} else if (top >= lineHeight && top >= lineHeight - margin) {    /* 20~25 */
return 2;
} else {    /* ~20 */
return 1;
}
},
sendLog: function (e) {
e.stopPropagation();
var target = function () {
if (e.target.tagName.toLowerCase() == "span") {
return e.target.firstChild;
} else if (e.target.tagName.toLowerCase() == "a") {
return e.target;
}
}();
var log = jq(target).data("log");
var extra = {
"relkwd": {
"click_query": jq(target).text()
}
};
smartLog(target, log, e, extra);
}
};
var netizenToggle;
netizenToggle = new NetizenToggle(position);
netizenToggle.init();
/* 이미지 탭에서 상단 관련검색어 미들 top 사이즈 체크할 때, 렌더링 타이밍 이슈로 넣어 둠. */
setTimeout(function () {
netizenToggle.setListType();
}, 0);
},
applyRight: function () {
/* ie6, ie7, ipad 가 아니면 */
if (!((SF.ua.browser.name == "msie" && (SF.ua.browser.version.major == "6" || SF.ua.browser.version.major == "7")) || (SF.ua.browser.name == "ipad"))) {
this.fixTop();
}
var listKeywords = jq("#netizenColl_right .list_keyword a.link_txt");
listKeywords.unbind("click").bind("click", jq.proxy(this.sendLog, this));
},
sendLog: function (e) {
e.stopPropagation();
var target = function () {
if (e.target.tagName.toLowerCase() == "span") {
return e.target.parentNode;
} else if (e.target.tagName.toLowerCase() == "a") {
return e.target;
}
}();
var log = jq(target).data("log");
var freeLog = {
"relkwd": {
"click_query": jq(target).text()
}
};
smartLog(target, log, e, freeLog);
},
fixTop: function () {
var netizenEl = jq("#netizenColl_right")[0];
if (netizenEl) {
var bodyHeight = jq("#daumWrap")[0].clientHeight;
if (viewsite == "0001L") {
/* SA일경우 */
var headerHeight = jq("#bingHead")[0].clientHeight;
var footerHeight = jq("#bingFoot")[0].clientHeight;
} else {
var headerHeight = jq("#daumHead")[0].clientHeight;
var footerHeight = jq("#daumFoot")[0].clientHeight;
}
var netizenHeight = netizenEl.clientHeight;
var netizenTop = jq(netizenEl).position().top;
var offset = 60;
/* 우하단 맨위로 버튼으로 인한 오프셋  */
var prevHeight = 0;
var browserHeight = 0;
var checkNetizen = function () {
var isHorizontalScrollbar = document.documentElement.scrollWidth > document.documentElement.clientWidth;
var scrollTop = getScrollOffsets().top;
browserHeight = getWindowSize().height;
var fixMode = ((scrollTop - headerHeight) >= netizenTop) ? true : false;
if (isHorizontalScrollbar) {
fixMode = false;
}
if (fixMode) {
jq(netizenEl).addClass("netizen_fixed");
if (scrollTop > (bodyHeight - (netizenHeight + footerHeight + offset))) {
netizenEl.style.top = bodyHeight - (footerHeight + offset + netizenHeight) - scrollTop + "px";
} else {
netizenEl.style.top = "-1px";
}
} else {
jq(netizenEl).removeClass("netizen_fixed");
}
};
var getScrollOffsets = function () {
return {
'left': window.pageXOffset || document.documentElement.scrollLeft || document.body.scrollLeft,
'top': window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop || document.body.scrollTop
};
};
var getWindowSize = function () {
var w = (window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth || document.body.clientWidth || 1003) - 2,
h = (window.innerHeight || document.documentElement.clientHeight || document.body.clientHeight || 650) - 2;
return {"width": w, "height": h};
};
checkNetizen();
jq(window).scroll(checkNetizen);
jq(window).resize(function () {
/* 브라우저 리사이즈시에는 높이가 달라졌을때는 클래스 순간 지움. (위치 새로 잡기위해) */
if (prevHeight == browserHeight) {
jq(netizenEl).removeClass("netizen_fixed");
}
checkNetizen();
prevHeight = browserHeight;
});
}
}
};
/**
* pc 우측 박스용 말줄임
*/
C.netizenColl.ellipsis = {
FRONT_MARGIN: 0,
ADDITIONAL_MARGIN: 15,
/**
1. 25byte 이상인 서브키가 몇개인지 측정
2. 그 글자들과 메인키의 일치비율 측정 => 편집거리 사용.
2-1. 키워드와 똑같이 잘라서 편집거리 측정
3. 일치비율 >= 0.5 이상이면 중간말줄임, 아니면 기본 말줄임
*/
draw: function () {
var _this = this;
var keyword = decodeURIComponent(utf8Query).replace(/\s/g, "");
var longKeyword = this.getLongSubkey();
if (longKeyword.length > 0) {
var editDistances = jq.map(longKeyword, function (subkey) {
/* 2-1 단계 */
var cuttingSubkey = subkey.replace(/\s/g, "").substring(0, keyword.length);
return _this.getEditDistance(_this.hangulToJaso(keyword), _this.hangulToJaso(cuttingSubkey));
});
var sumOfEditDistances = 0;
jq.each(editDistances, function (index, value) {
sumOfEditDistances += value;
});
var avgOfEditDistances = sumOfEditDistances / editDistances.length;
var zeroCnt = jq.grep(editDistances, function (dist) {
return dist <= avgOfEditDistances;
}).length;
var sumOfDiffSquare = 0;
jq.each(editDistances, function (index, dist) {
sumOfDiffSquare += Math.pow(dist - avgOfEditDistances, 2);
});
var matchRatio = zeroCnt / longKeyword.length;
var variance = sumOfDiffSquare / editDistances.length;
/* 일치비율이 0.5 이상이거나 0.3 이상이지만 분산이 2보다 작을때는 중간 말줄임 적용(프로그램명 n회 같은 쿼리는 일치비율이 작게 나오기 때문) */
if (matchRatio >= 0.5 || (matchRatio >= 0.3 && variance < 2)) {
this.setMiddleEllipsis();
} else {
this.setFullSubkey();
}
} else {
this.setFullSubkey();
}
},
/**
* 25byte 이상인 키워드 몇개인지 측정
*/
getLongSubkey: function () {
var _this = this;
return jq.map(jq("#netizenColl_right .txt_keyword"), function (elem, index) {
var subkey = jq(elem).attr("data");
if (_this.getByte(subkey) >= 25) {
return subkey;
}
});
},
/**
* 한글도 2byte로 계산하는 바이트 계산 함수
*/
getByte: function (s, b, i, c) {
for (b = i = 0; c = s.charCodeAt(i++); b += c >> 7 ? 2 : 1);
return b;
},
/**
* 한글 자소 분리
* brunch B.Util.js 의 hangulToJaso 가져와서 사용.
*/
hangulToJaso: function (text) {
var ChoSeong = [0x3131, 0x3132, 0x3134, 0x3137, 0x3138,
0x3139, 0x3141, 0x3142, 0x3143, 0x3145, 0x3146, 0x3147, 0x3148,
0x3149, 0x314a, 0x314b, 0x314c, 0x314d, 0x314e];
var JungSeong = [0x314f, 0x3150, 0x3151, 0x3152, 0x3153,
0x3154, 0x3155, 0x3156, 0x3157, 0x3158, 0x3159, 0x315a, 0x315b,
0x315c, 0x315d, 0x315e, 0x315f, 0x3160, 0x3161, 0x3162, 0x3163];
var JongSeong = [0x0000, 0x3131, 0x3132, 0x3133, 0x3134,
0x3135, 0x3136, 0x3137, 0x3139, 0x313a, 0x313b, 0x313c, 0x313d,
0x313e, 0x313f, 0x3140, 0x3141, 0x3142, 0x3144, 0x3145, 0x3146,
0x3147, 0x3148, 0x314a, 0x314b, 0x314c, 0x314d, 0x314e];
var chars = [];
var v = [];
for (var i = 0; i < text.length; i++) {
chars[i] = text.charCodeAt(i);
if (chars[i] >= 0xAC00 && chars[i] <= 0xD7A3) {
var i1, i2, i3;
i3 = chars[i] - 0xAC00;
i1 = i3 / (21 * 28);
i3 = i3 % (21 * 28);
i2 = i3 / 28;
i3 = i3 % 28;
v.push(String.fromCharCode(ChoSeong[parseInt(i1)]));
v.push(String.fromCharCode(JungSeong[parseInt(i2)]));
if (i3 != 0x0000)
v.push(String.fromCharCode(JongSeong[parseInt(i3)]));
}
else {
v.push(String.fromCharCode(chars[i]));
}
}
return v.join("");
},
/**
* 편집거리 측정
*/
getEditDistance: function (a, b) {
if (a.length === 0) return b.length;
if (b.length === 0) return a.length;
var matrix = [];
/* increment along the first column of each row */
var i;
for (i = 0; i <= b.length; i++) {
matrix[i] = [i];
}
/* increment each column in the first row */
var j;
for (j = 0; j <= a.length; j++) {
matrix[0][j] = j;
}
/* Fill in the rest of the matrix */
for (i = 1; i <= b.length; i++) {
for (j = 1; j <= a.length; j++) {
if (b.charAt(i - 1) == a.charAt(j - 1)) {
matrix[i][j] = matrix[i - 1][j - 1];
} else {
matrix[i][j] = Math.min(matrix[i - 1][j - 1] + 1, /* substitution */
Math.min(matrix[i][j - 1] + 1, /* insertion */
matrix[i - 1][j] + 1)); /* deletion */
}
}
}
return matrix[b.length][a.length];
},
/**
* 중간 말줄임 적용
*/
setMiddleEllipsis: function () {
var width = 0;
width = (jq("#netizenColl_right .list_keyword").width()) / 2;
if (width <= 0) {
this.setFullSubkey();
return;
}
width = width - this.FRONT_MARGIN - this.ADDITIONAL_MARGIN;
/* width 보다 넓으면 한글자씩 빼기 */
jq.each(jq("#netizenColl_right .txt_keyword"), function (index, elem) {
var subkey = jq(elem).attr("data");
var len = subkey.length;
jq(elem).text(subkey);
var mid = len / 2;
var removeLen = 2;
var head, tail;
while (jq(elem).width() > width) {
head = subkey.substring(0, mid - removeLen / 2);
tail = subkey.substring(mid + removeLen / 2, len);
jq(elem).text(head + "..." + tail);
removeLen++;
}
});
},
setFullSubkey: function () {
jq.each(jq("#netizenColl_right .txt_keyword"), function (index, elem) {
var subkey = jq(elem).attr("data");
jq(elem).text(subkey);
});
}
};
jq(document).ready(function () {
if (jq("#netizenColl_top").length > 0) {
C.netizenColl.applyTopBottom("top");
}
if (jq("#netizenColl_bottom").length > 0) {
C.netizenColl.applyTopBottom("bottom");
}
if (jq("#netizenColl_right").length > 0) {
C.netizenColl.applyRight();
C.netizenColl.ellipsis.draw();
}
});
})(jQuery);
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
(function () {
jq("#dirtColl .link_kakao").click(function (event) {
var parent = jq('#dirtColl .layer_kakao');
if (parent.hasClass('hide')) {
parent.removeClass('hide');
} else {
parent.addClass('hide');
}
});
jq("#dirtColl button.btn_close").click(function (event) {
var parent = jq('#dirtColl .layer_kakao');
if (parent.hasClass('hide')) {
parent.removeClass('hide');
} else {
parent.addClass('hide');
}
});
// jq("#dirtColl button.btn_close .btn_comm").click(function (event) {
// var parent = jq('.layer_kakao');
// if (parent.hasClass('hide')) {
// parent.removeClass('hide');
// } else {
// parent.addClass('hide');
// }
// });
jq("#dirtColl .wrap_search .box_search .tf_keyword").on('keyup', function () {
var box_field = jq("#dirtColl .wrap_search .box_search");
if (jq(this).val() != '') {
box_field.addClass('fld_on');
} else {
box_field.removeClass('fld_on');
}
});
jq("#dirtColl .wrap_search .box_search .tf_keyword").each(function () {
var box_field = jq("#dirtColl .wrap_search .box_search");
if (jq(this).val() != '') {
box_field.addClass('fld_on');
} else {
box_field.removeClass('fld_on');
}
});
})();
SF.C.directLinkColl = {
swipeContElem: jQuery('#dirtColl .rwd_list'),
previewSideBar: jQuery('#dirtColl .paging_nav'),
searchInput: jQuery('#dirtColl .wrap_search .box_search .tf_keyword'),
previewPageNum: 1,
redirectSearch: function (firstLinkUrl) {
if (firstLinkUrl != "") {
window.open(firstLinkUrl);
smartLog(null, 'dc=0DL&pg=1&rc=1&r=1&p=99&at=link&d=10E4iL3T4mOaHAyTZx', event);
}
},
previewPage: function (target) {
var root = this;
if (target == 'prev') this.previewPageNum = Math.max(1, this.previewPageNum - 1);
if (target == 'next') this.previewPageNum = Math.min(0, this.previewPageNum + 1);
this.previewSideBar.find('.emph_num').text(this.previewPageNum);
jQuery.getJSON("/qsearch?w=site&n=5&q=국방부&url=http://www.mnd.go.kr/&service=site^web&uk=" + uk + "&mk=" + mk + "&viewtype=json&p=" + this.previewPageNum, function (data) {
var result = data['RESULT']['SITE_PREVIEW']['ds'];
var preview_c = data['RESULT']['SITE_PREVIEW']['m']['total_count'];
jQuery.each(root.swipeContElem.find('li'), function (i, li) {
var $li = jQuery(li);
if (result[i] != undefined) {
$li.show();
$li.find('a').attr('href', result[i]['url']);
$li.find('img').attr('src', result[i]['thumbnail']);
$li.find('.tit_item').html(result[i]['title']);
var docid = result[i]['docid'];
var logP = 'dc=0DL&d=' + docid + '&pg=1&r=' + (5 * (root.previewPageNum - 1) + i + 1) + '&p=41&rc=' + preview_c + '&at=link';
$li.find('.link_item').attr('onclick', '').unbind('click').click(function () {
return smartLog(this, logP, event, { "cpid" : { "value" : "site^web" } });
});
} else {
$li.hide();
}
var btnPrev = jQuery("#btn_prev");
var btnNext = jQuery("#btn_next");
if(0 > 1) {
if (root.previewPageNum <= 1) {
if (!btnPrev.hasClass('btn_off'))
btnPrev.addClass('btn_off');
if (btnNext.hasClass)
btnNext.removeClass('btn_off');
} else if (root.previewPageNum == 0) {
if (btnPrev.hasClass)
btnPrev.removeClass('btn_off');
if (!btnNext.hasClass('btn_off'))
btnNext.addClass('btn_off');
} else {
if (btnPrev.hasClass)
btnPrev.removeClass('btn_off');
if (btnNext.hasClass('btn_off'))
btnNext.removeClass('btn_off');
}
}
});
root.webPreviewPageAccess = false;
});
},
onSearchSubmit: function (form) {
var siteUrl = 'http://mnd.go.kr';
if (siteUrl !== '') {
var detailQuery = this.searchInput.val();
form.q.value = 'site:' + siteUrl + ' ' + detailQuery;
var uParam = 'https://search.daum.net/search?w=web&q=' + form.q.value + "&detail_query=" + detailQuery;
smartLog(this, 'dc=0DL&d=10E4iL3T4mOaHAyTZx&pg=1&e=3&at=link&rc=0&u=' + encodeURIComponent(uParam), event, { "cpid" : { "value" : "site^web" } });
form.submit();
}
return false;
}
};
</script>  <div class="line"></div>
